aapaki car dub sakati he to kaaphi kuch batch saktaa tha
 Therefore, we have to go beyond water level towards flood forecast and storm water forecast, only then we can save loss of life and property
 hamen yah bhi bataanaa hoga ki baadh kaa pani aapke ilaake main kab tak rahegaa
 The comments madhya pradesh or rajasthan se baadh kii sthiti main sudhaar kii khabar he yani pani kaa str kam hone laga he
 Satna and Rewa were the most affected by floods in Madhya Pradesh
 udhar uttar pradesh main elahabaad, mirzapur, varanasi, mahoba, banda or unnav ke kai ilaakon main baadh ai hui he
 The Ganges and its tributaries are flowing above the danger mark here
 varanasi main ganga ke pani main aasapaas ke ghat duube hue hai
 Due to the sinking of Manikarnika Ghat and Harishchandra Ghat, cremation of dead bodies is now being done above the ghats here
 yahaan tak ki ganga aarti bhi chhaton par ho rahi he
 The Varuna River is also in spate in Varanasi, affecting ten thousand families around it
 elahabaad main bhi ganga kaa pani rihaayshi ilaakon main ghus gaya he
 When you too used to write in exams remembering very hard that there is a flood, then the fertile silt comes from the mountains towards the plains
 poshak tatwon se las mitti kii nai parat ban jaati he
 When we asked Professor Vishwas Kale of Pune, he said that flooding is an important part of the life process of the river
 baadh ke bagair nadi kaa jivan chakra puraa nahin hota he
 The fertility of the fields increases considerably due to the new soil that comes with the flood
 yahi vajah he ki hazaron saal se ganga-yamuna ke maidan main kheti ho rahi he, lekin vahaan kii urvartaa kabhi kam nahin hui
 The country's population of 500 million lives in the ganges-yamuna Plain
 yahi nahin baadh aane se nadi kaa channel lagaataar clear hota rahata he
 The large or small rivers bring with them sediments, sand-stones in normal times and accumulate around the edges, making the river channel narrower and shallower, reducing the water flow in the rivers
 jab badi baadh aati he to wo is puri gaad ko aage le jaati he or nadiyon ke channel ko saafe karti rahati he
 The river, which has been narrowed as a drain, re-spreads
 uske jin kinaaron par ret mafia se lekar bhu mafia tak kaa kabja ho chukaa hota he, un ilaakon ko nadi kii baadh ek jatke main hi mukt kara detii he
 The flooding causes the underground water recharge in the vicinity of the rivers, which serve the water needs during the rest of the year
 jitne bade ilaake main baadh aegi, utane ilaake main pani richarge hoga
 We spoke to Professor Dinesh Mishra who has studied life on the flood
 bahut kam log hai jo baadh par shodh karte hai
 i wanted them to come in 'prime time', but they had to go on a journey today
 jab maine pro mishra se poocha ki kya baadh aapadaa he, tabaahi he, to unka jawaab tha ki bihar ke liye baadh aapadaa nahin he
 If disaster had happened, it would have wreaked havoc, the density of population in Bihar would have been much lower
 log rajya chhod kar chale jate
 One does not leave his land because Bihar's land is fertile due to this flood
 yahaan pani kaa str acha he, isiilie aap haryana yaa rajasthan kii tarah mahilaon ko sir par gagari liye dur se pani laate-jate nahin dekhte hai
 Prof
 Mishra said that flooding is a profitable business
 bihar main 9 saal baad aisi baadh ai he, jisase yahaan kii zamin phir se nai ho gai he
 When Kosi was flooded, Anupam Mishra wrote an article - Swimming society is sinking
 unka kahana tha ki baadh atithi nahin he
 She does not come suddenly, but the date for her arrival is fixed
 yahi kaaran he ki jab baadh aati he tab ham uske saath vipatti kii tarah vyavhaar karte hai
 Anupam Mishra wrote that imagine how people would have protected themselves from floods when there were no governments, no helicopters, because the land on which they have lived has been flooding for centuries
 ham baadh ke raste main jaakar based hai, baadh hamaare raste main kabhi nahin aati he
 Why do floods cause havoc ek kaaran yah he ki ham sabane nadi ke kinare kii zamin par atikaraman kar liya he
 Since there is no flood for many years, we think that the flood will never come
 phir ham nadiyon ko tarah-tarah se jodne ke idia par kaam karne lagate hai
 Some have their minds fixed
 magar ek din baadh aa jaati he
 Now ask why there is loss of life and property
 kya ise bachaaya ja saktaa he
 You know that floods are being predicted in India since the days of Baba Adam
 yah bhavishyavaanee khatare ke nishaan ke aadhaar par kii jaati he
 You must have also heard in the news that if the water of Ganga or Punpun is flowing so much centimeter above the danger mark, then there will be flood
 desh main kareeb 175 jagahon par aise khatare ke nishaan bane hai jiske aadhaar par baadh kii bhavishyavaanee kii jaati he
 This system is called gauge to gauge correlation
 jaise aapane suna ki patna main ganga kaa pani khatare ke nishaan se upar bah rahaa he
 For this, the water level is measured at another place about sixty-seventy km ago
 iskaa ek aitihaasik data hota he, jiske aadhaar par kah diya jaataa he ki agar vahaan pani khatre ke nishaan se upar he to patna ke mahendru ghat yaa el si tii ghat main baadh kaa pani aa jayega
 If you are an old visitor of Patna, remember how we and you used to go to Bamboo Ghat or Mahendru Ghat as a child, to see how many stairs have reached the water
 agar itani seedhi tak pani aa gaya to baadh kaa pani shahar main ghus jayega
 This clearly shows that the system of measuring the risk of flooding from the water level must have become part of public life
 isse sateek bhavishyavaanee hoti hogi tabhi sarkaar se lekar aam naagarik tak is bhavishyavaanee main bharosa karte hai
 When the radio announcer used to say in a hoarse voice that the water level of the Ganges in Patna was flowing ten centimeters above the danger mark
 itnaa sunate hi log aalu pyaaz lekar chat par chale jate the
 It was seen in the sky that the chopper would drop some gram and biscuits
 magar dhire-dhire baadh kii sari tasviren tabaahi kii hone lagi
 People started dying, houses started sinking and how much was destroyed
 aisa kyon hua
 We spoke to another person in the area
 unka kahana he ki bharat main water level forcast kii vyavastha he yani jalastr ke aadhaar par bhavishyavaanee kii jaati he
 India should now forecast flood, that is, it should tell how long flood water will come in your area, how high it will rise and how long it will last
 aisa shaayad duniya ke baaki deshon main hota he
 Alerts start five to six days in advance
 agar bharat main flud forcast hota to chennai main baadh se saikadon log nahin marate, log apane hi makaan main dub kar nahin marate
 If we have to stop the damage caused by floods, then we have to step towards flood forecasts
 is vakt jalastr kii bhavishyavaanee central water kamishan karata he
 There is a limit to the prediction of water level
 aap pachaas-saath kimi ke bich do jagahon par khatre ke nishaan ko maapte hai, lekin agar bich main achaanak se pani aa jaae or aasapaas ke ilaake main fail jaae to uski bhavishyavaanee kii koi vyavastha nahin he
 For example, suppose the water level in the river bordering Chennai increased but due to heavy rains, the amount of water in the city increased from the other side
 ab iskaa hisaab lagaakar bataane kii vyavastha honi chahie ki chennai main kitni gaharaai tak baadh aane vaali he
 Therefore, people who are staying in the first floor house will have to go to the roof of at least two floors
 yah nahin hota he
 The second drawback is that we do not forecast storm water
 starm water varsha ke pani ko kehete hai
 It is a kind of urban flood
 jahaan nadiyaan nahin hoti he vahaan, starm water se baadh aati he
 If we can tell on the basis of the amount of rainfall that there will be so much millimeter of rain in Gurgaon or Delhi, then the roads can get filled with water
 aapaki car dub sakati he to kaaphi kuch batch saktaa tha
 Therefore, we have to go beyond water level towards flood forecast and storm water forecast, only then we can save loss of life and property

 aap pachaas-saath kimi ke bich do jagahon par khatre ke nishaan ko maapte hai, lekin agar bich main achaanak se pani aa jaae or aasapaas ke ilaake main fail jaae to uski bhavishyavaanee kii koi vyavastha nahin he

 The Tejas Express running between Delhi and Lucknow may be the first private train in the country
 iarsitisi ko do trainen lij par di jaaengi or ye trainen privet operators ko chalaane ke liye di ja sakati hai
 It is planned to run these trains on regular track with better passenger facilities on the lines of Palace on Wheels
 iarsitisi in donon trainon ke liye iarepasi ko lij chargees degi
 According to railway sources, it is likely that the previously announced Tejas train for Lucknow and Anand Vihar and the previously announced Tejas train between Chandigarh and New Delhi will be included in this experiment
 yah donon tejas express 2016 se railway ke time teble main shaamil hai, lekin ab tak inako chalaaya nahin gaya he yah donon railgadiyaan taiyaar hokar aa chuki hai
 The Tejas Express between Anand Vihar and Lucknow has been standing for the last one year
 railway ke adhikariyon ke mutabik iarsitisi in donon trainon ko apane paas lene ke baad nilaamee karke privet players yaa tourism agencys ko de sakati he
 This entire plan is yet to be made DPR
 gauratlab he ki railway ne 100 din ke agenda ko aage badhaate hue shuruaati taur par kuch train nijee haathon main saunpane kaa nirnay liya he
 The National Federation of Indian Railway Men (NFIR) has alleged that the budget has revealed that the government wants to move 'aggressively' on the corporatisation and privatization of railways
 eiroplen jaisi suvidhaayentejas desh kii pehali aisi train he jo 200 kilometre prati ghante kii raftaar ke liye ekadam feet he

 3 crore 25 lakh to make each and every compartment of Tejas Express
 tejas express desh main chalane vaali pehali aisi train hogi jisamen swachaalit plag tip daravaaje lagaae gaye hai
 That is, when the train runs, its doors will be closed automatically in the same manner as the doors of the metro train are closed
 chalati train main hi daravaaje nahin khulenge jab train rukegi tabhi yah daravaaje khul paaenge
 Tejas has been equipped with special and beautiful looking vinyl to give the train a special look
 puri train par ek khaas tarah kaa pattern chapa gaya he or iskaa color ugte hue suraj kii tarah rakhaa gaya he
 The Tejas train is named for staying sharp like the rays of the sun
 ise open biding ke proces ke baad privet player ko saunp diya jayega
 Privatization with the recommendation of the Bibek Debroy Committee To speed up privatization of Indian Railways, a seven-member committee was set up in September 2014 under the chairmanship of Niti Aayog member and economist Bibek Debroy
 is cameti kii draft report main hi suzav diya gaya tha ki bhartiya rail ke saath pratispardhaa ke liye nijee kshetra ko sawari tathaa maal gaadiyaan chalaane kii anumati deni chaiye, rail sambandhit aadharbhoot sevaayen tathaa utpaadan or nirmaan kaary jaise kaam, jo railway ke liye moolbhoot nahin hai, unamem nijee kshetra ke sahbhaag ko protsaahan diya janaa chahie
 Saturday was also a day of protest in Delhi

 is din ko gita jayanti (gita Jayanti) ke naam se janaa jaataa he

 Out of 18 chapters of Srimad Bhagavad Gita, there is the preaching of Karmayoga in the first 6 chapters, then Jnana Yoga in the next 6 chapters and Bhakti Yoga in the last 6 chapters
 gita jayanti ke din hi mokshada ekadshi (mokshada Ekadashi) bhi padati he
 It is believed that keeping this fast on this Ekadashi opens the doors of heaven to the dead ancestors of humans
 kehete hai ki jo bhi vyakti moksh paane kii ichha rakhata he use is ekadshi (ekadashi) par vrath rakhana chahie
